     <br class="cbo"> 
     <div class="sectionheader"> 
      <h2>Moderators</h2> 
     </div> 
     <div class="sectionbody"> 
      <div class="sectionbody-full"> 
       <p> We believe moderation starts with the community itself, so in addition to privileges earned through reputation, each site periodically holds <a href="http://blog.stackoverflow.com/2010/12/stack-exchange-moderator-elections-begin/">democratic moderator elections</a>. If the site is not yet large enough to support an election, we will <a href="http://blog.stackoverflow.com/2010/07/moderator-pro-tempore/">appoint moderators</a> from within the community. </p> 
       <p> Please see <a href="http://blog.stackoverflow.com/2009/05/a-theory-of-moderation/">Theory of Moderation</a> for information on our moderation philosophy. </p> 
      </div> 
     </div>
